     . .. .         ..  \n\nAfter much deliberation, the CPMhas named M Swaraj as its candidate for the upcoming Nilambur byelection. Swaraj, a former MLA from Thripunithura, lost the 2021 Assembly election to senior Congress leader  K. Babu by a narrow margin of 1,232 votes. He previously served as the Kerala State Secretary of both the StudentsFederation of India (SFI) and the Democratic Youth Federation of India (DYFI). The bypoll was necessitated by the resignation of sitting legislator PV Anvar, who parted ways with Chief Minister Pinarayi Vijayan on several issues.\n\nThe by-election is scheduled for June 19.
